When the `/work-on-task` command is invoked, you will:\n    36\t\n    37\t1. **Immediately switch to TDD mode**\n    38\t2. **Focus exclusively on the specified task**\n    39\t3. **Follow strict TDD methodology**\n    40\t4. **Ensure all acceptance criteria become passing tests**\n    41\t5. **Provide clear, executable code**\n    42\t\n    43\t### TDD Workflow Implementation\n    44\t\n    45\t#### Phase 1: GitHub Issue Analysis & Setup\n    46\t```\n    47\tSTEP 1: Fetch GitHub Issue\n    48\t- Retrieve issue details via GitHub API/CLI\n    49\t- Parse issue title, description, and acceptance criteria\n    50\t- Extract technical specifications and requirements\n    51\t- Identify linked issues and dependencies\n    52\t- Check current issue status and assignee\n    53\t\n    54\tSTEP 2: Repository Setup\n    55\t- Verify local repository state and remote connection\n    56\t- Create feature branch (if --branch specified)\n    57\t- Update issue status to \"in-progress\" (optional)\n    58\t- Add assignee and labels as needed\n    59\t- Post comment indicating work has started\n    60\t```\n    61\t\n    62\t#### Phase 2: Acceptance Criteria Mapping\n    63\t```\n    64\tSTEP 3: Parse Issue Requirements\n    65\t- Extract \"Acceptance Criteria\" section from issue\n    66\t- Convert checkboxes into testable scenarios\n    67\t- Identify \"Definition of Done\" requirements\n    68\t- Map technical specifications to implementation tasks\n    69\t- Plan test data and mock requirements\n    70\t```\n    71\t\n    72\t#### Phase 2: Red Phase (Failing Tests)\n    73\t```\n    74\tSTEP 3: Write Failing Tests\n    75\t- Create test files with descriptive names\n    76\t- Implement tests for each acceptance criterion\n    77\t- Include unit tests, integration tests as needed\n    78\t- Ensure all tests fail initially (Red phase)\n    79\t- Add test documentation and comments\n    80\t```\n    81\t\n    82\t#### Phase 3: Green Phase (Minimal Implementation)\n    83\t```\n    84\tSTEP 4: Implement Minimal Code\n    85\t- Write the simplest code to make tests pass\n    86\t- Focus on functionality, not optimization\n    87\t- Implement only what's needed for green tests\n    88\t- Avoid over-engineering or premature optimization\n    89\t```\n    90\t\n    91\t#### Phase 4: Refactor Phase (Code Improvement)\n    92\t```\n    93\tSTEP 5: Refactor & Optimize\n    94\t- Improve code structure and readability\n    95\t- Remove duplication and technical debt\n    96\t- Optimize performance where necessary\n    97\t- Maintain 100% test coverage\n    98\t- Update documentation\n    99\t```\n   100\t\n   101\t#### Phase 5: GitHub Integration & Completion\n   102\t```\n   103\tSTEP 6: Final Validation & Git Integration\n   104\t- Run complete test suite and ensure all tests pass\n   105\t- Verify all acceptance criteria checkboxes completed\n   106\t- Validate code quality and standards compliance\n   107\t- Stage all changes for commit\n   108\t\n   109\tSTEP 7: Commit & Push Changes\n   110\t- Generate comprehensive commit message with issue reference\n   111\t- Commit all changes with conventional commit format\n   112\t- 117\t- Link PR to original issue (auto-closes on merge)\n   118\t- Apply appropriate labels and request reviewers\n   119\t- Update issue with PR reference and completion status\n   120\t- Post final completion comment to issue\n   121\t```\n   122\t\n   123\t---\n   124\t\n   125\t## Output Format\n   126\t\n   127\t### 1. GitHub Issue Summary\n   128\t```markdown\n   129\t## Working on GitHub Issue #[Number]: [Issue Title]\n   130\t\n   131\t**Repository**: [owner/repo]\n   132\t**Assignee**: [Current assignee]  \n   133\t**Milestone**: [Target milestone]\n   134\t**Labels**: [Applied labels]\n   135\t**Epic**: [Related epic if applicable]\n   136\t\n   137\t### Issue Description\n   138\t[Original issue description]\n   139\t\n   140\t### Acceptance Criteria Analysis\n   141\t- ✅ [Checkbox 1]: [Description and test approach]\n   142\t- ✅ [Checkbox 2]: [Description and test approach]  \n   143\t- ✅ [Checkbox 3]: [Description and test approach]\n   144\t\n   145\t### Technical Specifications Identified\n   146\t- **API Changes**: [Endpoints to modify/create]\n   147\t- **Database Changes**: [Schema modifications needed]\n   148\t- **Testing Requirements**: [Unit, integration, E2E tests]\n   149\t- **Security Considerations**: [Auth, validation, etc.]\n   150\t\n   151\t### Implementation Strategy\n   152\t[Brief explanation of TDD approach for this specific issue]\n   153\t\n   154\t### Git Branch Strategy\n   155\t**Branch**: `feature/issue-[number]-[brief-description]`\n   156\t**Base Branch**: [main/develop/etc.]\n   157\t```\n   158\t\n   159\t### 2. TDD Implementation Phases\n   160\t\n   161\t#### Red Phase: Failing Tests\n   162\t```markdown\n   163\t### 🔴 RED PHASE: Writing Failing Tests\n   164\t\n   165\t**Test File**: `tests/[feature-name].test.js`\n   166\t\n   167\t```javascript\n   168\t// Test implementation\n   169\tdescribe('[Feature Name]', () => {\n   170\t  it('should [specific behavior]', () => {\n   171\t    // Test code that fails initially\n   172\t  });\n   173\t});\n   174\t```\n   175\t\n   176\t**Test Results**: ❌ [Number] tests failing (Expected)\n   177\t```\n   178\t\n   179\t#### Green Phase: Minimal Implementation\n   180\t```markdown\n   181\t### 🟢 GREEN PHASE: Minimal Implementation\n   182\t\n   183\t**Implementation File**: `src/[feature-name].js`\n   184\t\n   185\t```javascript\n   186\t// Minimal code to pass tests\n   187\tclass FeatureName {\n   188\t  // Implementation\n   189\t}\n   190\t```\n   191\t\n   192\t**Test Results**: ✅ [Number] tests passing\n   193\t```\n   194\t\n   195\t#### Refactor Phase: Code Improvement\n   196\t```markdown\n   197\t### 🔵 REFACTOR PHASE: Code Optimization\n   198\t\n   199\t**Refactored Code**: \n   200\t- Improved [specific aspect]\n   201\t- Extracted [common functionality]\n   202\t- Optimized [performance aspect]\n   203\t\n   204\t**Final Test Results**: ✅ All tests passing\n   205\t**Code Coverage**: [Percentage]%\n   206\t```\n   207\t\n   208\t### 3. GitHub Issue Updates & Progress Tracking\n   209\t```markdown\n   210\t## 📊 GitHub Issue Progress Updates\n   211\t\n   212\t### Initial Status Update\n   213\t**Comment Posted to Issue #[number]**:\n   214\t```\n   215\t🚀 **Starting TDD Implementation**\n   216\t\n   217\t**Branch**: `feature/issue-[number]-[description]`\n   218\t**Approach**: Test-Driven Development\n   219\t**Acceptance Criteria**: [X] total identified\n   220\t\n   221\t**Implementation Plan**:\n   222\t1. ✅ Red Phase: Write failing tests for all acceptance criteria\n   223\t2. 🔄 Green Phase: Implement minimal code to pass tests  \n   224\t3. ⏳ Refactor Phase: Optimize and clean up code\n   225\t4. ✅ Validation: Verify all requirements met\n   226\t\n   227\t**Progress**: 0% - Starting implementation\n   228\t```\n   229\t\n   230\t### Progress Updates During Implementation\n   231\t**Red Phase Complete**:\n   232\t```\n   233\t🔴 **Red Phase Complete** - All tests written and failing as expected\n   234\t\n   235\t**Tests Created**:\n   236\t- [X] Unit tests for [component/feature]\n   237\t- [X] Integration tests for [API endpoints]\n   238\t- [X] Edge case tests for [error scenarios]\n   239\t\n   240\t**Next**: Green Phase - Implementing minimal code to pass tests\n   241\t**Progress**: 25% - Tests established\n   242\t```\n   243\t\n   244\t**Green Phase Complete**:\n   245\t```\n   246\t🟢 **Green Phase Complete** - All tests now passing\n   247\t\n   248\t**Implementation Summary**:\n   249\t- [X] [Feature 1] implemented and tested\n   250\t- [X] [Feature 2] implemented and tested\n   251\t- [X] Error handling implemented\n   252\t\n   253\t**Code Coverage**: [X]%\n   254\t**Next**: Refactor Phase - Code optimization and cleanup  \n   255\t**Progress**: 75% - Core functionality complete\n   256\t```\n   257\t\n   258\t### 4. Final Commit & Pull Request Creation\n   259\t```markdown\n   260\t## 🚀 Implementation Complete - Creating PR\n   261\t\n   262\t### Final Commit Message\n   263\t```bash\n   264\tgit add .\n Rules\n   463\t\n   464\t### GitHub Issue Integration\n   465\t1. **Issue Validation**: Verify issue exists and is accessible\n   466\t2. **Permission Check**: Ensure write access to repository\n   467\t3. **Status Management**: Update issue status appropriately\n   468\t4. **Branch Creation**: Create feature branch following naming conventions\n   469\t5. **Progress Tracking**: Post regular updates to issue comments\n   470\t\n   471\t### Repository Requirements\n   472\t1. **Git Repository**: Must be in a valid git repository\n   473\t2. **GitHub Remote**: Repository must have GitHub remote configured\n   474\t3. **Authentication**: GitHub CLI authenticated with PR creation permissions\n   475\t4. **Branch Permissions**: Ability to create branches and open PRs\n   476\t5. **Clean Working State**: All changes properly staged for final commit\n   477\t\n   478\t### Issue Format Requirements\n   479\t1. **Acceptance Criteria**: Issue must contain testable acceptance criteria\n   480\t2. **Technical Specs**: Implementation details should be provided\n   481\t3. **Definition of Done**: Clear completion requirements\n   482\t4. **Proper Labels**: Appropriate type and component labels\n   483\t\n   484\t### TDD Enforcement Rules\n   485\t1. **Always start with failing tests**: No implementation before tests\n   486\t2. **Test every acceptance criterion**: 1:1 mapping minimum\n   487\t3. **Incremental development**: Small, focused commits during development\n   488\t4. **Continuous validation**: Run tests after each change\n   489\t5. **Final commit**: Single comprehensive commit with all changes\n   490\t6. **Automatic PR**: Create pull request with detailed description\n   491\t7. **Issue closure**: Link PR to issue for automatic closure on merge\n   492\t\n   493\t---\n   494\t\n   495\t## Example Usage Scenarios\n   496\t\n   497\t### Scenario 1: Simple Issue Implementation\n   498\t```bash\n   499\t/work-on-task 123\n   500\t```\n   501\t**Expected Workflow**:\n   502\t1. **Fetch Issue**: Gets GitHub Issue #123 from current repository\n   503\t2. **Branch Creation**: `feature/issue-123-jwt-auth-middleware`\n   504\t3. **Status Update**: Issue labeled \"in-progress\", comment posted\n   505\t4. **TDD Implementation**: Red → Green → Refactor cycle\n   506\t5. **Progress Updates**: Regular comments on issue with progress\n   507\t6. **Final Commit**: Comprehensive commit with all changes\n   508\t7. **PR Creation**: Auto-generated PR with detailed description\n   509\t8. **Issue Update**: Final completion comment with PR link\n   510\t\n   511\t### Scenario 2: Cross-Repository Issue\n   512\t```bash\n   513\t/work-on-task myorg/backend#456\n   514\t```\n   515\t**Expected Workflow**:\n   516\t1. **Repository Switch**: Validates access to `myorg/backend`\n   517\t2. **Issue Analysis**: Fetches issue #456 from specified repository\n   518\t3. **Local Setup**: Ensures local repo is synced with remote\n   519\t4. **Implementation**: Standard TDD workflow with cross-repo issue updates\n   520\t5. **PR Creation**: Pull request created in correct repository\n   521\t6. **Cross-Reference**: Original issue updated with PR link\n   522\t\n   523\t### Scenario 3: Custom Branch with Auto-PR\n   524\t```bash\n   525\t/work-on-task 789 --branch=feature/auth-jwt-tokens\n   526\t```\n   527\t**Expected Workflow**:\n   528\t1. **Custom Branch**: Creates specified branch name instead of auto-generated\n   529\t2. **Issue Linking**: Links custom branch to issue #789\n   530\t3. **Implementation**: Normal TDD workflow with custom branch\n   531\t4. **Auto-Commit**: Final commit with comprehensive message\n   532\t5. **PR Creation**: Pull request from custom branch with auto-generated description\n   533\t6. **Reviewer Assignment**: Automatic reviewer assignment based on issue labels\n   534\t\n   535\t### Scenario 4: Epic Sub-task with Complete Workflow\n   536\t```bash\n   537\t/work-on-task 234\n   538\t# Where #234 is part of Epic #200\n   539\t```\n   540\t**Expected Workflow**:\n   541\t1. **Epic Context**: Recognizes issue is part of larger epic\n   542\t2. **Implementation**: Standard TDD implementation\n   543\t3. **Final Commit**: Commit message references both issue and epic\n   544\t4. **PR Creation**: PR description includes epic context\n   545\t5. **Epic Updates**: Updates epic progress when PR is created\n   546\t6. **Milestone Tracking**: Updates milestone progress automatically\n   547\t7. **Team Notification**: Notifies epic stakeholders of completion\n   548\t\n   549\t---\n   550\t\n   551\t## Error Handling\n   552\t\n   553\t### GitHub Issue Not Found\n   554\t```\n   555\t❌ Error: Issue #123 not found in current repository.\n   556\tAvailable options:\n   557\t- Check issue number: /work-on-task 124\n   558\t- Specify repository: /work-on-task myorg/repo#123\n   559\t- List open issues: gh issue list\n   560\t```\n   561\t\n   562\t### Repository Access Issues\n   563\t```\n   564\t❌ Error: No access to repository 'myorg/backend'.\n   565\tPlease check:\n   566\t- Repository exists and is accessible\n   567\t- GitHub authentication: gh auth login\n   568\t- Repository permissions (read/write required)\n   569\t```\n   570\t\n   571\t### Issue Format Problems\n   572\t```\n   573\t❌ Error: Issue #123 missing acceptance criteria.\n   574\tGitHub Issues must include:\n   575\t- Clear acceptance criteria (checkboxes)\n   576\t- Technical specifications\n   577\t- Definition of done\n   578\t\n   579\tPlease update issue format or use /create-issues to generate properly formatted issues.\n   580\t```\n   581\t\n   582\t### Branch Creation Conflicts\n   583\t```\n   584\t❌ Error: Branch 'feature/issue-123-auth' already exists.\n   585\tOptions:\n   586\t1. Switch to existing branch: git checkout feature/issue-123-auth\n   587\t2. Use different branch: /work-on-task 123 --branch=feature/auth-v2\n   588\t3. Delete existing branch: git branch -D feature/issue-123-auth\n   589\t```\n   590\t\n   591\t### PR Creation Failures\n   592\t```\n   593\t❌ Error: Failed to create pull request.\n   594\tPossible causes:\n   595\t- No changes to commit (all acceptance criteria already implemented)\n   596\t- Branch protection rules prevent PR creation\n   597\t- Missing required reviewers or approvals\n   598\t- GitHub API rate limit exceeded\n   599\t\n   600\tSolutions:\n   601\t- Verify changes exist: git status\n   602\t- Check branch protection: gh repo view --web\n   603\t- Retry with --force flag: /work-on-task 123 --force-pr\n   604\t```\n   605\t\n   606\t### Commit Message Generation Issues\n   607\t```\n   608\t⚠️  Warning: Unable to generate comprehensive commit message.\n   609\tUsing fallback commit message format.\n   610\t\n   611\tFallback commit:\n   612\t```\n   613\tfeat: implement issue #123\n   614\t\n   615\t- Complete TDD implementation\n   616\t- All acceptance criteria met\n   617\t- Tests passing\n   618\t\n   619\tCloses #123\n   620\t```\n   621\t\n   622\tRecommendation: Review and amend commit message before push.\n   623\t```\n   624\t\n   625\t---\n   626\t\n   627\t## Integration Notes\n   628\t\n   629\t### GitHub CLI Requirements\n   630\t- **GitHub CLI**: `gh` command must be installed and authenticated\n   631\t- **Repository Access**: Read/write permissions to target repository\n   632\t- **API Tokens**: Personal access token with repo and issues scope\n   633\t\n   634\t### Git Repository Setup\n   635\t- **Valid Git Repo**: Must be run from within a git repository\n   636\t- **GitHub Remote**: Repository must have GitHub remote configured\n   637\t- **Clean Working Directory**: Uncommitted changes should be stashed\n   638\t\n   639\t### Commit Message Integration\n   640\t```bash\n   641\t# Automatic commit message format\n   642\tgit commit -m \"feat: implement JWT auth middleware\n   643\t\n   644\t- Add token validation middleware\n   645\t- Implement user role checking\n   646\t- Add comprehensive error handling\n   647\t\n   648\tCloses #123\"\n   649\t```\n   650\t\n   651\t### Pull Request Integration\n   652\t```markdown\n   653\t# Auto-generated PR description template\n   654\t## Description\n   655\tImplements GitHub Issue #[number]: [issue title]\n   656\t\n   657\t## criteria tests passing\n   664\t- Code coverage: [percentage]%\n   665\t- [Security/Performance] review completed\n   666\t\n   667\t## Related Issues\n   668\tCloses #[issue-number]\n   669\tPart of Epic #[epic-number] (if applicable)\n   670\t\n   671\t## Checklist\n   672\t- [x] All tests passing\n   673\t- [x] Code review completed\n   674\t- [x] Documentation updated\n   675\t- [x] Security considerations addressed\n   676\t```\n   677\t\n   678\t### Advanced PR Features\n   679\t```bash\n   680\t# Automatic reviewer assignment based on CODEOWNERS\n   681\tgh pr create --reviewer \"@team/backend,@security-lead\"\n   682\t\n   683\t# Auto-assign labels based on issue labels\n   684\tgh pr create --label \"enhancement,security,backend\"\n   685\t\n   686\t# Link to milestone and project boards\n   687\tgh pr create --milestone \"v2.0\" --project \"Backend Development\"\n   688\t\n   689\t# Draft PR for work-in-progress (optional flag)\n   690\t/work-on-task 123 --draft-pr\n   691\t```\n   692\t\n   693\t### Framework Support\n   694\t- **JavaScript**: Jest, Mocha, Cypress\n   695\t- **Python**: pytest, unittest, nose2\n   696\t- **Java**: JUnit, TestNG, Mockito\n   697\t- **C#**: NUnit, xUnit, MSTest\n   698\t- **Go**: testing package, Ginkgo\n   699\t- **Rust**: built-in test framework\n   700\t\n   701\t### Continuous Integration\n   702\t- Tests should be executable in CI/CD pipeline\n   703\t- Coverage reports should be generated automatically\n   704\t- Failed tests should block deployment\n   705\t\n   706\t---\n   707\t\n   708\t## Best Practices\n   709\t\n   710\t### GitHub Issue Workflow\n   711\t1. **Issue Assignment**: Assign yourself when starting work\n   712\t2. **Branch Naming**: Use consistent `feature/issue-[number]-[description]` format\n   713\t3. **Regular Updates**: Post progress comments every major milestone\n   714\t4. **Atomic Commits**: Each commit should reference the issue number\n   715\t5. **Quality Gates**: Ensure all acceptance criteria pass before completion\n   716\t\n   717\t### Complete Workflow Integration\n   718\t1. **Implementation Phase**: TDD cycle with incremental commits\n   719\t2. **Final Validation**: Comprehensive test suite and acceptance criteria check\n   720\t3. **Code Consolidation**: Stage all changes for single comprehensive commit\n   721\t4. **Commit Creation**: Generate detailed commit message with conventional format\n   722\t5. **Branch Push**: Push feature branch to GitHub remote\n   723\t6. **PR Generation**: Create pull request with auto-generated description\n   724\t7. **Issue Completion**: Update original issue with PR link and completion status\n   725\t8. **Team Notification**: Notify relevant team members and reviewers\n   726\t\n   727\t### Automated Quality Gates\n   728\t1. **Test Coverage**: Ensure minimum coverage threshold met\n   729\t2. **Security Scan**: Run security linting and vulnerability checks  \n   730\t3. **Code Standards**: Validate code formatting and conventions\n   731\t4. **Documentation**: Verify API docs and README updates completed\n   732\t5. **Performance**: Run performance benchmarks if applicable\n   733\t\n   734\t### Post-Implementation Automation\n   735\t```bash\n   736\t# Automatic actions after PR creation\n   737\t- Issue status updated to \"ready-for-review\"\n   738\t- Epic progress updated (if sub-task)\n   739\t- Milestone progress calculated\n   740\t- Team notifications sent\n   741\t- CI/CD pipeline triggered\n   742\t- Code quality reports generated\n   743\t```\n   744\t\n   745\t### Code Quality & Collaboration\n   746\t1. **Clear Communication**: Detailed progress comments for team visibility\n   747\t2. **Security First**: Address security considerations in acceptance 68\t\n    69\t## API Usage\n    70\t\n    71\t### Generate Video\n    72\t```bash\n    73\tcurl -X POST http://localhost:8080/api/v1/videos \\\n    74\t  -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n 93\t\n    94\tVideoCraft uses a comprehensive JSON configuration format:\n    95\t\n    96\t```json\n    97\t{\n    98\t  \"comment\": \"Example video configuration\",\n    99\t  \"resolution\":  136\t        }\n   137\t      ]\n   138\t    }\n   139\t  ]\n   140\t}\n   141\t```\n   142\t\n   143\t## Architecture Overview\n   144\t\n   145\t```mermaid\n   146\tgraph TB\n   147\t    Client[Client] --> API[HTTP API Layer]\n   148\t    API --> Auth[Auth Middleware]\n   149\t    API --> JobSvc[Job Service]\n   150\t    \n   151\t    JobSvc --> AudioSvc[Audio Service]\n   152\t    JobSvc --> TransSvc[Transcription Service]\n   153\t    JobSvc --> SubSvc[Subtitle Service]\n   154\t    JobSvc --> FFmpegSvc[FFmpeg Service]\n   155\t    JobSvc --> StorageSvc[Storage Service]\n   156\t    \n   157\t    TransSvc --> Daemon[Python Whisper Daemon]\n   158\t    SubSvc --> ASSGen[ASS Generator]\n   159\t    FFmpegSvc --> FFmpeg[FFmpeg Binary]\n   160\t    \n   161\t    AudioSvc --> FFprobe[FFprobe Analysis]\n   162\t    StorageSvc --> FileSystem[File System]\n   163\t```\n   164\t\n   165\t### Core Components\n   166\t\n   167\t- **HTTP API Layer**: RESTful endpoints with Gin framework\n   168\t- **Job Service**: Async job processing and queue management  \n   169\t- **Audio Service**: Audio file analysis and duration calculation\n   170\t- **Transcription Service**: Go-Python daemon communication for Whisper AI\n   171\t- **Subtitle Service**: ASS subtitle generation with progressive timing\n   172\t- **FFmpeg Service**: Video encoding with command injection prevention\n   173\t- **Storage Service**: File management and cleanup\n   174\t\n   175\t## Progressive Subtitles Deep Dive\n   176\t\n   177\tVideoCraft's progressive subtitle system provides word-level timing accuracy:\n   178\t\n   179\t### How It Works\n   180\t1. **Audio Analysis**: Extract real audio file duration using FFprobe\n   181\t2. **Scene Timing**: Calculate precise scene start/end times based on audio durations\n   182\t3. **Transcription**: Python Whisper daemon generates word-level timestamps\n   183\t4. **Timing Mapping**: Map Whisper relative timestamps to absolute video timeline\n   184\t5. **ASS Generation**: Create styled subtitle file with word-by-word timing\n   185\t\n   186\t### Key Innovation\n   187\tUnlike simple concatenation approaches, VideoCraft uses **real audio file durations** instead of transcription speech durations for scene timing, ensuring continuous playback without gaps.\n   188\t\n   189\t## Development\n   190\t\n   191\t### Project Structure\n   192\t```\n   193\tvideocraft/\n   194\t├── cmd/                    # Entry points (server, CLI)\n   195\t├── internal/\n   196\t│   ├── api/               # HTTP configs\n   203\t```\n   204\t\n   205\t### Building\n   206\t```bash\n   207\t# Development build\n   208\tmake build\n   209\t\n   210\t# Production build\n   211\tmake build-prod\n   212\t\n 43\tANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your_anthropic_api_key_here\n    44\t\n    45\t# GitHub token (automatically provided)\n    46\tGITHUB_TOKEN=${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}\n    47\t```\n    48\t\n    49\t### 234\t```\n   235\t\n   236\t### Adjust Sensitivity\n   237\t\n   238\t```yaml\n   239\t# Modify trigger sensitivity\n   240\ttriggers:\n   241\t  documentation_changes: \"always\"  # always,
